Was recommended to me. I drove from the city of Tulare. I had a great experience! Josh, the smog tech, took care of me and he was very professional and provided prompt service.  First impression was a clean shop and a smile from Josh.  I have automotive experience and a lot of other smog places I have gone to try to do more than one thing at a time. He gave me and my vehicle his undivided attention. He inspected my car and tested it. I was in and out as it should be. After he finished he went over the results and highlighted the good of my emissions results but also the things I should keep an eye on. <UserId.>111136072805631619412</UserId.><name>Paul Conrad</name><date>1422337060758< /date>< rating>
3<//rating>
< Text>
Be very cautious with Royal Computers. While I have no reason to doubt the quality of their work, I experienced a bate and switch on pricing that was worrisome to say the least. I brought my damaged laptop in for a diagnostic and was originally quoted $325. This seemed reasonable, so I gave the go ahead.

After a few delays out of Royal's control (I got a call saying that a wrong part had been sent from a supplier and they had to wait for a new one), I finally got a call saying my laptop was ready but the technician recommended an operating system reinstall. Assuming this was complementary, I said yes. Anyone who has a Mac knows the operating system is now a free download and is very simple to install.  In any event, when I called to arrange for pickup the next day I was informed the bill was $675.

Note: no one had ever asked me to approve additional expenses beyond the initial estimate. The most ludicrous charge was $150 for the operating system reinstall. In their defense, and this is why I am giving them three stars instead of one, Royal Computers adjusted the bill after I pointed out to them that I had not approved additional expenses. The front desk staff was courteous and seemed to understand my frustration. Apparently it was the owner who stepped in to make things right, which I appreciate, though I never spoke with him directly.

Maybe my experience was a fluke. In the very least, though, you should be very careful if you take your computer to Royal to ask them to have you approve any additional expenses beyond the initial estimate. Also, don't have them reinstall your operating system. $150 to reinstall Mac OS X is like a car mechanic charging you $150 to air up your tires.</Text>
